[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer run against the AVIF library’s YUV-to-RGB conversion code triggers an [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer error for a dynamic stack buffer overflow. The overflow occurs in [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mreformat.[0m[1;92mc:812[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during a read of four bytes outside [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe bounds of a stack-allocated buffer. The issue surfaces when exercising the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mYuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert harness.[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – During fuzzing, AddressSanitizer detects a dynamic-stack-buffer-overflow in the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` at `src/libavif/src/reformat.[0m[1;92mc:812:46[0m[39m`.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – A [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte read occurs beyond the allocated stack frame, leading to memory [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorruption and a crash.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – The stack trace shows propagation through `avifImageYUVToRGBImpl` and the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpublic API function `avifImageYUVToRGB`, invoked by the fuzz harness’s `Convert` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroutine.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – Stack-based buffer overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdynamic stack overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the YUV-to-RGB [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreformatting logic.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The overflow is specifically flagged as a “dynamic-stack-buffer-overflow,” [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicating use of a variable-length or alloca’d buffer whose bounds are [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmiscalculated.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The offending code resides in the slow-path converter [0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, rather than in the fast SIMD paths.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The test harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`YuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m supplies arbitrary image [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparameters and data to the reformatter, exposing the out-of-bounds read.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The buffer overflow occurs consistently at the same source location when [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing certain fuzz-generated inputs.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Affected Code Areas  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – `src/libavif/src/reformat.c`  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    * Function: `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow`  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    * Related functions: `avifImageYUVToRGBImpl`, `avifImageYUVToRGB`  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  – Fuzz test harness  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    * File: `src/libavif/tests/gtest/avif_fuzztest_yuvrgb.cc`  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    * Routine: `[0m[1;35mConvert[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which allocates and populates an `avifImage`, then [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcalls the conversion API.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m• Recommended Investigation Focus  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Examine the buffer allocation and indexing logic in [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow`, especially around line [0m[1;36m812[0m[39m in `reformat.c`.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Review the way row pointers, line strides, and subsampling factors determine [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer size.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Audit any use of dynamic stack allocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., alloca or C99 VLAs[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconversion code.  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Correlate the parameters generated by `YuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdimensions, chroma sampling, flags[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with the computed buffer extents.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Trace how edge cases in chroma subsampling or image dimensions might lead to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder-sized stack buffers.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m796[0m[39m:                    total_spill += [0m[1;35mfabs[0m[1;39m([0m[39mspill_Cr[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m797[0m[39m:                    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m if spill too high, dampen[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m798[0m[39m:                    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->height * image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m >= [0m[1;36m0x1000[0m[39m && total_spill[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m> [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mimage->height * image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m3.[0m[39m8f[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m799[0m[39m:                        int a, b;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m800[0m[39m:                        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m801[0m[39m:                            a = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m802[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39melse[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m803[0m[39m:                            a = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m804[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m805[0m[39m:                        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m == [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m{[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m806[0m[39m:                            b = [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m807[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m}[0m[39melse[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m808[0m[39m:                            b = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m809[0m[39m:                        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m810[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m811[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m812[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m813[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m814[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m815[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m816[0m[39m:                        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m817[0m[39m:                        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi+a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj+b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m818[0m[39m:                    [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m   [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m819[0m[39m:                [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m820[0m[39m:            [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The dynamic-stack-buffer-overflow in `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow` stems from [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munguarded indexing of two C99 VLAs [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mwidth[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mheight[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mwidth[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mheight[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. In the “spill dampening” loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m810[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffsets `a` and `b` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mderived from `adjCol`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`adjRow`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m can be +[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m at the right/bottom [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimage boundary, causing reads/writes one past the end of those VLAs.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Core Logic  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We keep the original spill‐generation algorithm intact, preserving the “slow” [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreference path for arbitrary down-[0m[35m/[0m[95mup-sampling.[0m[39m  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We do not modify the public API signatures, fuzz harness, or utility functions[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39manywhere else in the codebase.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We retain the VLA approach [0m[1;39m([0m[39mso the code structure and performance [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacteristics remain unchanged[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, adding just safety checks around out-of-bounds [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneighbors.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Outline  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Enhance boundary checks for both positive- and negative-offset neighbors:  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Immediately after computing the two-offset variables—call them `a` [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mhorizontal[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `b` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvertical[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m—insert clamps for negative underflow:  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m existing: a = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : +[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;  b = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj % [0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m : +[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mi + a < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m a = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mint[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mj + b < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m b = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi + [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint32_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39ma >= image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m a = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj + [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint32_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mb >= image->height[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m b = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; [0m[1;39m}[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        This mirrors the existing positive-side guards [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbut written portably with [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msigned casts for the negative side[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so `a` and `b` will always land in `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwidth-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, height-[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` respectively when added to `i`[0m[35m/[0m[39m`j`.  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Around lines [0m[1;36m810[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m818[0m[39m, wrap each neighbor access in an `if` that verifies [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mits index remains in-bounds before dereferencing:  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m current pixel always safe[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m   -= pSpillCb;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m   -= pSpillCr;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m horizontal neighbor[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mi + [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint32_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39ma < image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi + a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi + a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m vertical neighbor[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj + [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint32_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mb < image->height[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj + b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj + b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m diagonal neighbor[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39mi + [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint32_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39ma < image->width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m &&[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;39m([0m[39mj + [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint32_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mb < image->height[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            uspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi + a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj + b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCb;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            vspill_image[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi + a[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m[[0m[39mj + b[0m[1;39m][0m[39m -= pSpillCr;[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. No changes are made to the test harness, fuzzing logic, or external [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdependencies.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. The added casts to `[0m[1;39m([0m[39muint32_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` ensure that the signed-to-unsigned conversion[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis well-defined for the bounds checks and that any negative offset [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif it somehow [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mslipped through[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is treated as “out-of-bounds” and skipped.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This minimal patch directly addresses the out-of-bounds read/write without [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrefactoring the entire spill array approach or migrating to heap allocations.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - It preserves the existing algorithm’s semantics for interior pixels and only [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodifies behavior at true image edges—edges that the original code already [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempted to clamp for positive overflow.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Fuzz-based tests will still drive arbitrary dimensions; with these guards in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mplace, neither negative underflow nor positive overflow can touch red zones.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigation  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Edge‐pixel spill contributions might differ very slightly [0m[1;39m([0m[39mneighboring [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontributions that would have wrapped around are now skipped[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This matches the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginal intent of clamping at boundaries.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The performance impact is negligible: only a handful of integer comparisons [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mper pixel.  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No new dependencies or file-wide changes are introduced; maintenance burden [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains low.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Validation  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run `YuvRgbFuzzTest.Convert` under AddressSanitizer: verify no [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdynamic-stack-buffer-overflow reports in `avifImageYUVAnyToRGBAnySlow`.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that all existing unit tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding gist-based image‐compare [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtests[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue to pass with identical outputs, except for expected minor edge-case[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdifferences.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCode Range to Patch:  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code_range>src/libavif/src/reformat.[0m[1;92mc:769[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m820[0m[39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_range[0m[39m>[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
